## קֵא (id: 006353000000000)

קֵא
===

קֵא (H6892a)

noun m · קיא

Body Products

vomit \= regurgitated food product; ≈ associated with something repugnant

[PRO 26:11](https://ref.ly/Prov26:11)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Proverbs 26:11


## קָאָת (id: 006354000000000)

קָאָת
=====

קָאָת (H6893) — קָאַת

noun f

Birds

jackdaw exact meaning unsure: \= relatively small black bird; ► unclean; ≈ associated with loneliness, devastation, destruction, and possibly death

[LEV 11:18](https://ref.ly/Lev11:18) · [DEU 14:17](https://ref.ly/Deut14:17) · [PSA 102:7](https://ref.ly/Ps102:7) · [ISA 34:11](https://ref.ly/Isa34:11) · [ZEP 2:14](https://ref.ly/Zeph2:14)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Leviticus 11:18; Deuteronomy 14:17; Psalms 102:7; Isaiah 34:11; Zephaniah 2:14


## קַב (id: 006355000000000)

קַב
===

קַב (H6894)

noun m · קבב

Capacity

kab \= unit of dry measure of approximately 2 liters; 6 kabs make up one seah; 18 kabs make up 1 ephah (ABD);

[2KI 6:25](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:25)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** 2 Kings 6:25


## קבב (id: 006356000000000)

קבב
===

קבב (H6895) [SAHD](https://sahd-online.com/words/q-b-b/)

verb · נקב · קַב · קֻבָּה

Curse 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ ארר · זעם 

|  |
| --- |

 ≠ ברך · בְּרָכָה

to curse \= causative action by which humans or deities consign humans to death, usually by invoking the name of a deity if the agent is human; ◄ this is done as punishment, out of contempt, fear, anger, or hostility, or because one was paid to do so; ► the effectiveness of a curse partially depends on the authority of the one pronouncing it

[NUM 22:11](https://ref.ly/Num22:11) · [NUM 22:17](https://ref.ly/Num22:17) · [NUM 23:8](https://ref.ly/Num23:8) · [NUM 23:8](https://ref.ly/Num23:8) · [NUM 23:11](https://ref.ly/Num23:11) · [NUM 23:13](https://ref.ly/Num23:13) · [NUM 23:25](https://ref.ly/Num23:25) · [NUM 23:25](https://ref.ly/Num23:25) · [NUM 23:27](https://ref.ly/Num23:27) · [NUM 24:10](https://ref.ly/Num24:10) · [JOB 3:8](https://ref.ly/Job3:8) · [JOB 5:3](https://ref.ly/Job5:3)1 · [PRO 11:26](https://ref.ly/Prov11:26) · [PRO 24:24](https://ref.ly/Prov24:24)

1 JOB 5:3 MT HOTTP\-B RSV NJPS NRSV GNT \| NIV NJB "to be cursed" \| REB "to be ruined"

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 22:11; Numbers 22:17; Numbers 23:8; Numbers 23:11; Numbers 23:13; Numbers 23:25; Numbers 23:27; Numbers 24:10; Job 3:8; Job 5:3; Proverbs 11:26; Proverbs 24:24


## קֵבָה (id: 006357000000000)

קֵבָה
=====

קֵבָה (H6896 · H6897) — קֹבָה

noun f

stomach, belly \= part of body; ◄ located in abdomen; ► location for the storage of food; ≈ sometimes used in a less exact sense to refer to the belly

[NUM 25:8](https://ref.ly/Num25:8) · [DEU 18:3](https://ref.ly/Deut18:3)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 25:8; Deuteronomy 18:3


## קֻבָּה (id: 006358000000000)

קֻבָּה
======

קֻבָּה (H6898)

noun f · קבב

Tents

inner room meaning unsure, possibly: \= inner room in a tent ► possibly the part reserved for women and the location where a man and woman had sex

[NUM 25:8](https://ref.ly/Num25:8)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 25:8

## קְבוּרָה (id: 006360000000000)

קְבוּרָה
========

קְבוּרָה (H6900)

noun f · קבר

Space

burial \= action by which the body of someone who died is laid down in a designated place, such as a hole in a rock or in the ground, or in a place which was constructed specifically for this purpose; ≈ not receiving a burial is considered a deep humiliation

[2CH 26:23](https://ref.ly/2Chr26:23) · [ECC 6:3](https://ref.ly/Eccl6:3) · [ISA 14:20](https://ref.ly/Isa14:20) · [JER 22:19](https://ref.ly/Jer22:19)

Tombs

tomb, grave \= place where one or more people are buried, such as a hole in a rock or in the ground, or a place which was constructed specifically for this purpose

[GEN 35:20](https://ref.ly/Gen35:20) · [GEN 35:20](https://ref.ly/Gen35:20) · [GEN 47:30](https://ref.ly/Gen47:30) · [DEU 34:6](https://ref.ly/Deut34:6) · [1SA 10:2](https://ref.ly/1Sam10:2) · [2KI 9:28](https://ref.ly/2Kgs9:28) · [2KI 21:26](https://ref.ly/2Kgs21:26) · [2KI 23:30](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:30) · [EZK 32:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek32:23) · [EZK 32:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek32:24)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** 2 Chronicles 26:23; Ecclesiastes 6:3; Isaiah 14:20; Jeremiah 22:19; Genesis 35:20; Genesis 47:30; Deuteronomy 34:6; 1 Samuel 10:2; 2 Kings 9:28; 2 Kings 21:26; 2 Kings 23:30; Ezekiel 32:23; Ezekiel 32:24


## קבל (id: 006361000000000)

קבל
===

קבל (H6901 · A6902)

verb · קְבֹל

Hold 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi

to take hold of, to receive, to accept \= action by which humans take hold of an object and accept responsibility for it

[2CH 29:16](https://ref.ly/2Chr29:16) · [2CH 29:22](https://ref.ly/2Chr29:22) · [EZR 8:30](https://ref.ly/Ezra8:30) · [EST 4:4](https://ref.ly/Esth4:4) · [DAN 2:6](https://ref.ly/Dan2:6)

Associate 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi

to receive, to welcome \= action by which humans receive other humans in their company

[1CH 12:19](https://ref.ly/1Chr12:19) · [1CH 12:19](https://ref.ly/1Chr12:19)

Bear 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ קום · שׁמע

to accept, to receive \= action by which humans accept an event with willingness and/or patience

[1CH 21:11](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:11) · [EST 9:23](https://ref.ly/Esth9:23) · [EST 9:27](https://ref.ly/Esth9:27) · [EST 9:27](https://ref.ly/Esth9:27) · [JOB 2:10](https://ref.ly/Job2:10) · [JOB 2:10](https://ref.ly/Job2:10) · [PRO 19:20](https://ref.ly/Prov19:20) · [DAN 6:1](https://ref.ly/Dan6:1) · [DAN 7:18](https://ref.ly/Dan7:18)

Space 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

to be opposite to, to correspond to \= state in which an object is located in a position opposite another, similar object

[EXO 26:5](https://ref.ly/Exod26:5) · [EXO 36:12](https://ref.ly/Exod36:12)

1 EST 9:27 MT\-K וקבל \| MT\-Q וְקִבְּלוּ

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** 2 Chronicles 29:16; 2 Chronicles 29:22; Ezra 8:30; Esther 4:4; Daniel 2:6; 1 Chronicles 12:19; 1 Chronicles 21:11; Esther 9:23; Esther 9:27; Job 2:10; Proverbs 19:20; Daniel 6:1; Daniel 7:18; Exodus 26:5; Exodus 36:12


## קְבֹל (id: 006362000000000)

קְבֹל
=====

קְבֹל (H6904 · H6905) — קָבָל, קֹבֶל

noun m · קבל

Weapons 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ חֶרֶב · כַּר

battering\-ram \= a log or other long, heavy piece of wood covered on one end with metal; it was rammed by soldiers against the wall or gate of a city under siege; it sometimes had a point since the purpose of the ramming was to wedge a hole in the wall; others were blunt on the end; it could be held and swung by soldiers, or sometimes it was suspended by ropes from a moveable wooden tower.

[EZK 26:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek26:9)

noun m · קבל

Space

before, in front of \= relation linking an event to the location right in front of an object

[2KI 15:10](https://ref.ly/2Kgs15:10)

1 2KI 15:10 MT HOTTP\-C NIV NJPS NRSV CEV \| RSV NJB REB GNT ביבלעם "in Ibleam" \= יִבְלְעָם

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Ezekiel 26:9; 2 Kings 15:10

Graham S. Ogden

 verb nif, verb hit

Gather 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb pi 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ אסף

to gather, to collect, to amass, to pick \= causative action by which humans gather inanimate objects from different sources to keep for oneself or store it

Compile 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to gather \= causative action by which humans gather different types of information in order to compile it into a story

Color 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi

**Collocation:** קבץ פָּארוּר

to grow pale literally: to gather (one's) flush; hence: \= process by which people have a reduced blood flow in the skin causing a lighter complexion, ◄ as a result of fear

## קַדִּישׁ (id: 006381000000000)

קַדִּישׁ
========

adj · קדשׁ

Holy

holy \= state in which a deity differs from humans and other deities in that he cannot be associated with anything that is in any way profane or tainted by sin or other impurities, which is a quality that he desires to see in everything else as well

set apart \> saint literally: holy one; hence: \= human being in the service of God and therefore set apart from other people

holy one \> angel literally; holy one; hence: \= supernatural being in the service of God

## קדם (id: 006382000000000)

קדם
===

קדם (H6923)

verb · קְדוּמִים · קָדִים · קֶדֶם · קַדְמָה · קִדְמָה · קַדְמֹון · קַדְמֹנִי · קֵדְמָה · קְדֵמֹות · קַדְמִיאֵל

Space 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi

to approach, to come before, to stand before, to confront \= action by which humans place themselves in front of individuals or groups, facing either forward or backward, ► and either with good or with evil intentions; ≈ sometimes used figuratively in situations where humans come before God in worship, or where God confronts enemies, or when certain conditions are personified

[2SA 22:19](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:19) · [PSA 17:13](https://ref.ly/Ps17:13) · [PSA 18:19](https://ref.ly/Ps18:19) · [PSA 68:26](https://ref.ly/Ps68:26) · [PSA 89:15](https://ref.ly/Ps89:15) · [PSA 95:2](https://ref.ly/Ps95:2) · [MIC 6:6](https://ref.ly/Mic6:6) · [MIC 6:6](https://ref.ly/Mic6:6)

Space 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi

to bring, to put in front of \= causative action by which humans place an object in front of another object

[2KI 19:32](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:32) · [ISA 37:33](https://ref.ly/Isa37:33)

Engage 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi

to be in action before (another event) literally: to come before (a moment in time); hence: \= action by which humans come into action before a certain event starts taking place ◄ as if meeting that event on its way

[PSA 119:147](https://ref.ly/Ps119:147) · [PSA 119:148](https://ref.ly/Ps119:148)

Engage 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi

to do something beforehand literally: to come before (another event, that might eventually take place); hence: \= action by which humans perform an event in haste before it can be prevented

[JON 4:2](https://ref.ly/Jonah4:2)

Meet 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi, verb hif

to meet, to receive, to welcome literally: to come before; hence: \= action by which humans meet other humans that are travelling from one location to another ► either with good or with evil intentions; ≈ often extended to describe certain events that happen in people's lives

[DEU 23:5](https://ref.ly/Deut23:5) · [2SA 22:6](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:6) · [NEH 13:2](https://ref.ly/Neh13:2) · [JOB 3:12](https://ref.ly/Job3:12) · [JOB 30:27](https://ref.ly/Job30:27) · [JOB 41:3](https://ref.ly/Job41:3)1 · [PSA 18:6](https://ref.ly/Ps18:6) · [PSA 21:4](https://ref.ly/Ps21:4) · [PSA 59:11](https://ref.ly/Ps59:11) · [PSA 79:8](https://ref.ly/Ps79:8) · [PSA 88:14](https://ref.ly/Ps88:14) · [ISA 21:14](https://ref.ly/Isa21:14) · [AMO 9:10](https://ref.ly/Amos9:10)

קֶדֶם
=====

noun m · קדם

Spatial Referents 

|  |
| --- |

 ≠ אָחֹור

in front \= a referent pointing in the direction that one is facing

[PSA 139:5](https://ref.ly/Ps139:5)

|  |
| --- |

## קדר (id: 006394000000000)

קדר
===

קדר (H6937)

verb · קַדְרוּת · קְדֹרַנִּית · קֵדָר · קִדְרֹון

Color 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb hit

to grow dark, to become dark \= process by which an object becomes dark in color

[1KI 18:45](https://ref.ly/1Kgs18:45) · [JOB 6:16](https://ref.ly/Job6:16) · [JOB 30:28](https://ref.ly/Job30:28)1

Dark 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal 

|  |
| --- |

 ≠ נֹגַהּ

to grow dark, to be darkened \= process by which celestial bodyies stop producing or reflecting light

[JOL 2:10](https://ref.ly/Joel2:10) · [JOL 4:15](https://ref.ly/Joel4:15) · [MIC 3:6](https://ref.ly/Mic3:6)

Dark 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ כסה · נתן חֹשֶׁךְ 

|  |
| --- |

 ≠ אור

to darken, to make dark \= causative action by which deities cause celestial bodies to stop producing or reflecting light

[EZK 32:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek32:7) · [EZK 32:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek32:8)

Dress 

|  |
| --- |

 Grieve 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ אבל · אָבֵל · אמל · עוה · שׁבר · שׁחח · שַׁמָּה · שָׁפָל

to mourn exact meaning unsure: \= action by which humans put on dark and/or dusty clothes; or: to wear a dark and gloomy expression on their face; ◄ caused by grief as a result of the death of a loved one, ill health, oppression, suffering, or compassion for someone else's suffering; ► in order to make it publicly known that one is mourning

[JOB 5:11](https://ref.ly/Job5:11) · [JOB 30:28](https://ref.ly/Job30:28)1 · [PSA 35:14](https://ref.ly/Ps35:14) · [PSA 38:7](https://ref.ly/Ps38:7) · [PSA 42:10](https://ref.ly/Ps42:10) · [PSA 43:2](https://ref.ly/Ps43:2) · [JER 4:28](https://ref.ly/Jer4:28) · [JER 8:21](https://ref.ly/Jer8:21) · [JER 14:2](https://ref.ly/Jer14:2)

Dress 

|  |
| --- |

 Grieve 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ עֻלְפֶּה

to cause to mourn exact meaning unsure: \= causative action by which deities cause humans to wear a dark and gloomy expression on their faces; ◄ caused by grief as a result of the death of a loved one, ill health, oppression, suffering, or compassion for someone else's suffering; ► in order to make it publicly known that one is mourning

[EZK 31:15](https://ref.ly/Ezek31:15)

1 JOB 30:28 RSV NIV \[a] \| NJPS NJB NRSV REB GNT CEV \[d]

Graham S. Ogden

## קדשׁ (id: 006399000000000)

קדשׁ
====

קדשׁ (H6942)

verb · מִקְדָּשׁ · קָדֹושׁ · קָדֵשׁ · קֹדֶשׁ · קַדִּישׁ

Innocent 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hit

to sanctify oneself, to consecrate oneself \= action by which humans that are part of a holy nation set themselves apart from others by not engaging in activities that are not in accordance with God's law

[LEV 11:44](https://ref.ly/Lev11:44) · [LEV 20:7](https://ref.ly/Lev20:7)

Holy 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi, verb hif, verb pu'al

to set apart, to dedicate, to consecrate \= causative action by which humans or deities set apart humans or objects for a particular purpose or activity relating to the service of God, as a result of which they become holy

## קֹדֶשׁ (id: 006402000000000)

קֹדֶשׁ
======

קֹדֶשׁ (H6944)

noun m · קדשׁ

Holy

holiness, holy \= state in which a deity differs from humans and other deities in that he cannot be associated with anything that is in any way profane or tainted by sin or other impurities, which is a quality that he desires to see in everything else as well

Buildings 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ דְּבִיר

(most) holy place \= innermost room at the back of the main temple building; ► location of the ark of the covenant; ≈ regarded as the most holy place

[LEV 16:2](https://ref.ly/Lev16:2) · [EZK 41:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek41:21) · [EZK 41:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek41:23)

Buildings 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ דְּבִיר

**Collocation:** קֹדֶשׁ הַקֳּדָשִׁים

most holy place literally: the holiest of holies; hence: \= innermost room at the back of the main temple building; ► location of the ark of the covenant; ≈ regarded as the most holy place

## קָדֵשׁ בַּרְנֵעַ (id: 006403000000000)

קָדֵשׁ בַּרְנֵעַ
================

קָדֵשׁ בַּרְנֵעַ (H6947)

name

Names of Locations 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ עֵין־מִשְׁפָּט · קָדֵשׁ · קֶדֶשׁ

Kadesh\-Barnea \= town, also known as En Mishpat , Kedesh, and Kadesh; ◄ located in the Wilderness of Zin, in the northern part of Sinai peninsula; ► Israelites encamped there on their way from Egypt to Canaan; it is also the location of the Meribah spring; spies were sent out into Canaan from this place; it later marked the southern border of the territory of Judah

[NUM 32:8](https://ref.ly/Num32:8) · [NUM 34:4](https://ref.ly/Num34:4) · [DEU 1:2](https://ref.ly/Deut1:2) · [DEU 1:19](https://ref.ly/Deut1:19) · [DEU 2:14](https://ref.ly/Deut2:14) · [DEU 9:23](https://ref.ly/Deut9:23) · [JOS 10:41](https://ref.ly/Josh10:41) · [JOS 14:6](https://ref.ly/Josh14:6) · [JOS 14:7](https://ref.ly/Josh14:7) · [JOS 15:3](https://ref.ly/Josh15:3)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 32:8; Numbers 34:4; Deuteronomy 1:2; Deuteronomy 1:19; Deuteronomy 2:14; Deuteronomy 9:23; Joshua 10:41; Joshua 14:6; Joshua 14:7; Joshua 15:3


## קהה (id: 006404000000000)

קהה
===

קהה (H6949)

verb

Impact 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to be blunt?, to be numb exact meaning unknown; \= process by which one's teeth are affected by the eating of sour grapes, and become blunt, numb, or adversely affected in another way

Impact 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi

to be blunt \= state in which a tool loses its sharp cutting edge, ◄ as a result of frequent use, ► so that it has become ineffective and needs sharpening

[ECC 10:10](https://ref.ly/Eccl10:10)

Sounds 

|  |
| --- |

 noun m pl

thunder literally: voices; hence: \= loud rumbling and crashing noises from heaven accompanying flashes of lightning; ≈ regarded as God's voice

[EXO 9:23](https://ref.ly/Exod9:23) · [EXO 9:28](https://ref.ly/Exod9:28) · [EXO 9:29](https://ref.ly/Exod9:29) · [EXO 9:33](https://ref.ly/Exod9:33) · [EXO 9:34](https://ref.ly/Exod9:34) · [EXO 19:16](https://ref.ly/Exod19:16) · [EXO 20:18](https://ref.ly/Exod20:18) · [1SA 12:17](https://ref.ly/1Sam12:17) · [1SA 12:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam12:18) · [JOB 28:26](https://ref.ly/Job28:26) · [JOB 38:25](https://ref.ly/Job38:25) · [PSA 93:4](https://ref.ly/Ps93:4)

Associate

**Collocation:** קֹול אֶחָד

in unison literally: one voice; hence: \= action by which a group of people do things in one accord

[EXO 24:3](https://ref.ly/Exod24:3) · [2CH 5:13](https://ref.ly/2Chr5:13)

Know

meaning literally: voice (of a sign); hence: \= something that is communicated by a certain event

Shout 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

**Collocation:** נשׂא קוֹל

to raise (one's) voice, to do (something) loudly literally: to lift up (one's) voice; hence: \= action by which humans raise their voice, ► either in order to shout or to speak

Shout 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

**Collocation:** רום קֹול

to shout literally: to raise (one's) voice; hence: \= action by which humans raise their voice. ► either in order to shout or to speak

Speak

report, news, proclamation literally: voice; hence: \= process by which information is passed on within a community

Speak 

|  |
| --- |

 verb pi

**Collocation:** חנן קֹול

to speak kindly, to speak charmingly literally: to make (one's) voice kind; hence: \= actions by which humans speak in a kind and gracious way ► in order to win a favorable attitude from other humans

[PRO 26:25](https://ref.ly/Prov26:25)

Know 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

**Collocation:** הלך קֹול

to carry (someone's) voice literally: to cause (someone's) voice to go; hence: \= causative action by which a bird passes on someone's words to another person

## קֹולָיָה (id: 006418000000000)

קֹולָיָה
========

קֹולָיָה (H6964)

name · קֹול · יהוה

Names of People

Kolaiah \= man; ◄ son of Maaseiah; tribe of Benjamin; ► ancestor of Sallu, after exile

[NEH 11:7](https://ref.ly/Neh11:7)

Names of People

Kolaiah \= man; ► father of Ahab, a false prophet in the time of Jeremiah

[JER 29:21](https://ref.ly/Jer29:21)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Nehemiah 11:7; Jeremiah 29:21

| --- |

Stance 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif, verb hof

Alive 

|  |
| --- |

 Strong

to restore literally: to rise up (to life); hence: \= process by which individuals or entire nations become healthy, strong, and/or prosperous after a time of misfortune

Alive 

|  |
| --- |

 Strong

to restore literally: to cause to rise up (to life); hence: \= causative process by which deities cause individuals or entire nations to be healthy, strong, and/or prosperous after a time of misfortune

Exist 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif, verb pi, verb haf'el, verb af'el

to raise, to erect, to set up, to put together, to build literally: to cause to arise; hence: \= causative action by which humans put a construction in place

Conflict 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb hit, verb pi

to rise up (against), to oppose, to attack literally: to arise (against someone); hence: \= action by which humans or animals approach (other) humans with the intention of opposing or fighting them

 verb qal, verb pe'al

to arise, to rise up, to take action, to set out, to leave, to prepare, to proceed literally: to arise; hence: \= action by which humans or deities get ready to engage in an action, which usually involves more than simply rising from a sitting or lying position and requires some preparation

Engage 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

to rouse, to stir up literally: to raise up; hence: \= caustive action by which deities cause humans to get ready to engage in an action, which usually involves more than simply rising from a sitting or lying position and requires some preparation

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

to carry out, to perform, to keep literally: to raise up (a commandment or promise); hence: \= action by which humans or deities engage in a particular action

 verb pi

Associate 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif

**Collocation:** קום לְעַם

Great 

|  |
| --- |

 verb hif, verb hof

Happen 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb pe'al

to arise, to happen, to come literally: to arise; hence: \= process by which an event starts taking place

## קָנֶה (id: 006513000000000)

קָנֶה
=====

קָנֶה (H7070)

noun m · קנה

Plants

reed \= a tall grass with stiff, sharply\-pointed leaves and a plume\-like flower head that reaches to more than 2 m; it grows in lakes and streams, the roots creeping across the bottom of the lake to produce new leaves and stalks; or on riverbanks; ◄ Phragmites australis (Common reed) or Arundo donax (Giant reed); ► used for baskets, mats, flutes, pens, arrows, and roof\-coverings; ≈ symbol of weakness and undependability, but also flexibility

[1KI 14:15](https://ref.ly/1Kgs14:15) · [2KI 18:21](https://ref.ly/2Kgs18:21) · [JOB 40:21](https://ref.ly/Job40:21) · [PSA 68:31](https://ref.ly/Ps68:31) · [ISA 19:6](https://ref.ly/Isa19:6) · [ISA 35:7](https://ref.ly/Isa35:7) · [ISA 36:6](https://ref.ly/Isa36:6) · [ISA 42:3](https://ref.ly/Isa42:3) · [EZK 29:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek29:6)

Plants 

|  |
| --- |

 Spices

fragrant grass, calamus, sweet flag meaning unsure; either: (1\) \= type of grass that grows in clumps to more than a meter high and has stiff leaves like sword grass and has a sweet smell; ◄ Cymbopogon; ► oil is extracted by boiling and distilling the leaves; used in the oil for anointing priests; or (2\) \= a type of reed with stiff leaves, distinguished by its green flower head that grows on a stalk to about 50 cm high; ◄ Acorus calamus or Calamus; ► the scented leaves and more strongly scented tubers have traditionally been used medicinally and to make fragrances, and the dried and powdered tubers have been used as a substitute for ginger, cinnamon and nutmeg

[EXO 30:23](https://ref.ly/Exod30:23) · [SNG 4:14](https://ref.ly/Song4:14) · [ISA 43:24](https://ref.ly/Isa43:24) · [JER 6:20](https://ref.ly/Jer6:20) · [EZK 27:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:19)

Tools

**Collocation:** קְנֵה מִדָּה

measuring reed, measuring stick \= reed used as a linear measure of six royal cubits, i.e. of 3\.1 meters

[EZK 40:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:3) · [EZK 40:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:5) · [EZK 40:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:5) · [EZK 40:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:5) · [EZK 40:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:6) · [EZK 40:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:6) · [EZK 40:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:7) · [EZK 40:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:7) · [EZK 40:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:7) · [EZK 40:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:8) · [EZK 41:8](https://ref.ly/Ezek41:8) · [EZK 42:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:16) · [EZK 42:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:16) · [EZK 42:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:16) · [EZK 42:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:17) · [EZK 42:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:17) · [EZK 42:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:18) · [EZK 42:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:18) · [EZK 42:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:19) · [EZK 42:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:19)

Shout 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb pe'al, verb pe'il, verb nif

to read, to recite \= action by which humans speak written words aloud

Great 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal ptc.pass, verb nif

to be renowned literally: to be called (by name); hence: \= state in which humans have a high reputation which results in their names being pronounced on a regular basis

[RUT 4:11](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:11) · [RUT 4:14](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:14) · [EZK 23:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek23:23)

Know 

|  |
| --- |

 verb nif

to be named, to be known literally: to be called; hence: \= state in which a person is known with certain characteristics and treated as such

[GEN 21:12](https://ref.ly/Gen21:12) · [GEN 48:6](https://ref.ly/Gen48:6) · [GEN 48:16](https://ref.ly/Gen48:16) · [1CH 23:14](https://ref.ly/1Chr23:14) · [EZR 2:61](https://ref.ly/Ezra2:61) · [NEH 7:63](https://ref.ly/Neh7:63) · [ISA 14:20](https://ref.ly/Isa14:20)

Know 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to proclaim, to make a proclamation literally: to cry out; hence: \= causative action by which humans or deities make a public announcement

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb nif, verb pu'al, verb hitpe'el

to call, to summon, to invite literally: to cry out; hence: \= causative action by which humans or deities let (other) humans know that they are to come, either by approaching them directly or sending a message

Happen 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to summon, to call for (an event) literally: to call, summon; hence: \= causative action by which deities cause certain things to happen, ◄ as if they were people that were summoned

[JER 25:29](https://ref.ly/Jer25:29) · [LAM 2:22](https://ref.ly/Lam2:22) · [EZK 38:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek38:21) · [HAG 1:11](https://ref.ly/Hag1:11)

Name 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb nif, verb pu'al

to name literally: to cry out; hence: \= action by which humans or deities assign a name to a person, place, object, or phenomenon

Name 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb nif, verb pu'al

**Collocation:** קרא שֵׁם

to name literally: to cry out (someone's) name (something); hence: \= action by which humans assign a name to a person or place

Associate 

|  |
| --- |

 verb nif

**Collocation:** קרא שֵׁם

to be called (by someone's name) literally: (one's) name is called (over someone); hence: \= state in which a person or building is closely associate to another person or a deity

Serve 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ ידע

**Collocation:** קרא בְּשֵׁם

to acknowledge (a deity) literally: to call on (someone's) name; hence: \= action by which humans acknowledge a deity and are willing to live in accordance with some of the requirements of that deity

[PSA 79:6](https://ref.ly/Ps79:6) · [PSA 80:19](https://ref.ly/Ps80:19) · [ISA 41:25](https://ref.ly/Isa41:25) · [ISA 64:6](https://ref.ly/Isa64:6) · [JER 10:25](https://ref.ly/Jer10:25) · [JOL 3:5](https://ref.ly/Joel3:5) · [ZEP 3:9](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:9)

Dissociate 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal ptc.pass

to choose, to elect literally: to cry out; hence: \= causative action by which a community selects leader by calling out their name

[NUM 1:16](https://ref.ly/Num1:16)

verb

Meet 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb nif

to meet \= action by which humans purposefully move in the direction of (another) human, deity, or object to engage with them

## קֹרֵא (id: 006563000000000)

קֹרֵא
=====

קֹרֵא (H6981 · H7124) — קֹורֵא

noun m · קרא

Birds

rock partridge, black francolin, sand partridge \= type of partridge, of which there were at least three variaties in ancient Israel; it lives in small flocks called coveys, lays a great many eggs, and prefers to run when in danger, flying only when necessary; even when it takes flight it flies for only a short distance before dropping back to the ground; habitat differs from one kind of partridge to another; the rock partridge is about 35 centimeters (14 inches) in length and has striking white cheeks with a black band running from its brow, through its eyes, down its neck, and curving around its breast; It also has striking black and chestnut stripes on its flanks; its back and wings are gray; the beak and legs are red; both sexes look alike; the black francolin is about the same size but has a slightly shorter tail; the male has a black breast and flanks; the female is a speckled brown; the sand partridge is the color of the local sand and is about half the size of the other two types; ◄ Alectoris graeca, Alectoris chukar, Francolinus francolinus, Ammoperdix heyi; ► clean animal, so may be eaten

[1SA 26:20](https://ref.ly/1Sam26:20) · [JER 17:11](https://ref.ly/Jer17:11)

name

Names of People

Kore \= man; ◄ son of Ebiasaph; tribe of Levi; ► father of Shallum, gatekeeper, after exile

[1CH 9:19](https://ref.ly/1Chr9:19)

Names of People

Kore \= man; ◄ descendant of Asaph; tribe of Levi; ► gatekeeper; time of king David

[1CH 26:1](https://ref.ly/1Chr26:1)

Names of People

Kore \= man; ◄ son of Jimnah; tribe of Levi; ► gatekeeper; time of king Hezekiah

[2CH 31:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr31:14)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** 1 Samuel 26:20; Jeremiah 17:11; 1 Chronicles 9:19; 1 Chronicles 26:1; 2 Chronicles 31:14


## קרב (id: 006564000000000)

קרב
===

קרב (H7126 · A7127)

verb · קְרָב · קָרֵב · קִרְבָה · קָרְבָּן · קֻרְבָּן · קָרֹוב

Move 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb pe'al, verb pi, verb hif, verb nif

## קְרָב (id: 006565000000000)

=====

קֶרֶב (H7130)

noun m

inner parts, entrails, stomach, womb \= the inner parts of the body of humans or animals, such as stomach, intestines, womb, etc.

Self

## קָרֵב (id: 006567000000000)

קָרֵב
=====

קָרֵב (H7131)

adj · קרב

Move

to approach, to come near, to come forward \= action by which humans move to a location relatively close to the location in focus

[NUM 1:51](https://ref.ly/Num1:51) · [NUM 3:10](https://ref.ly/Num3:10) · [NUM 3:38](https://ref.ly/Num3:38) · [NUM 17:28](https://ref.ly/Num17:28) · [NUM 17:28](https://ref.ly/Num17:28) · [NUM 18:7](https://ref.ly/Num18:7) · [DEU 20:3](https://ref.ly/Deut20:3) · [1SA 17:41](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:41) · [2SA 18:25](https://ref.ly/2Sam18:25) · [1KI 5:7](https://ref.ly/1Kgs5:7) · [EZK 40:46](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:46) · [EZK 45:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek45:4)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 1:51; Numbers 3:10; Numbers 3:38; Numbers 17:28; Numbers 18:7; Deuteronomy 20:3; 1 Samuel 17:41; 2 Samuel 18:25; 1 Kings 5:7; Ezekiel 40:46; Ezekiel 45:4


## קִרְבָה (id: 006568000000000)

קִרְבָה
=======

קִרְבָה (H7132)

noun f · קרב

Associate

drawing near (to God) literally: approaching (God); hence: \= process by which humans draw close to a deity by living according to his commands

[PSA 73:28](https://ref.ly/Ps73:28) · [ISA 58:2](https://ref.ly/Isa58:2)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 73:28; Isaiah 58:2

## קָרְחָה (id: 006581000000000)

קָרְחָה
=======

קָרְחָה (H7144)

noun f · קרח

Bald

bald spot \= a hairless patch on the head of an animal or human being in a location where hair normally grows; ≈ this can be a natural phenomenon, as on the head of a vulture, but it can also be created by shaving the head as a sign of mourning

## קֶרֶן (id: 006598000000000)

קֶרֶן
=====

קֶרֶן (H7161a · A7162)

noun f · קֶרֶן הַפּוּךְ · קֶרֶן הַפּוּךְ · קַרְנַיִם

Animals

horn \= outgrowth of bone encased in hardened skin, often curved and pointed, found in pairs on the heads of cattle, sheep, goats, and other animals; ► used for defending itself against aggression or for attacking other animals; ≈ associated with strength and honor; a raised horn symbolizes confidence and/or pride

 ≈ גַּלְגַּל · חֲשַׁשׁ · עָלֶה · עָפָר

stubble, chaff \= dry grass\-like remnant of wheat or another grain crop following the harvest; this term possibly refers to two kinds of material, one being the remnant of the crop remaining in the ground, the other being the unwanted residue of stalks; ► only used for brick making; ≈ usually considered of little value and needing to be separated from the grain itself; maybe burned

## קַשְׂקֶשֶׂת (id: 006632000000000)

קַשְׂקֶשֶׂת
===========

קַשְׂקֶשֶׂת (H7193)

noun f

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ סְנַפִּיר

scales \= small overlapping plates covering the body of a fish

[LEV 11:9](https://ref.ly/Lev11:9) · [LEV 11:10](https://ref.ly/Lev11:10) · [LEV 11:12](https://ref.ly/Lev11:12) · [DEU 14:9](https://ref.ly/Deut14:9) · [DEU 14:10](https://ref.ly/Deut14:10) · [EZK 29:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek29:4) · [EZK 29:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek29:4)

Clothing 

|  |
| --- |

 Weapons 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ כֹּובַע · מַד · קֹובַע

**Collocation:** שִׁרְיֹון קַשְׂקַשִּׂים

coat of mail \= a kind of vest or shirt covering the upper part of the body and made of several hundred small bronze scales or platelets overlapping each other and sewn on a cloth or leather base; the scales were thin and about 11 by 6 centimeters; such armor was lighter than a solid metal breastplate and was also more flexible, giving greater maneuverability; used especially by soldiers who could not carry a shield but still needed protection in battle (for example, a chariot driver).

[1SA 17:5](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:5)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Leviticus 11:9; Leviticus 11:10; Leviticus 11:12; Deuteronomy 14:9; Deuteronomy 14:10; Ezekiel 29:4; 1 Samuel 17:5
